I am a married mother with 3 kids. In the past I have utilized payday loan services in between pay datesto pay bills that were due and needed to be paid. I do have a bank account however I get charged $35 for each bounce fee iffunds are not avail. So to get a payday loan has been a solution I have used to only be charged 1 fee. As a mother I do not haveextra $ to pay out.
